        <div class="encoding-list">
            <template x-for="([fileName, file], index) in sortedFiles" :key="fileName">
                <div class="encoding-item" :id="file.isTooBig &amp;&amp; sortedFiles.filter(([fn, f]) =&gt; f.isTooBig).findIndex(([fn]) =&gt; fn === fileName) === 0 ? 'rejected-files' : null" :class="{
                        'encoding-item--error': file.status === 'error',
                        'encoding-item--success': file.status === 'success',
                        'encoding-item--processing': file.status !== 'success' &amp;&amp; file.status !== 'error',
                        'encoding-item--too-big': file.isTooBig
                    }" x-transition:enter="transition ease-out duration-200" x-transition:enter-start="opacity-0 transform scale-95" x-transition:enter-end="opacity-100 transform scale-100">
                    <div class="encoding-item-main" @click="if (file.status === 'success') file.showCode = !file.showCode" :style="file.status === 'success' ? 'cursor: pointer;' : ''">
                        <div class="encoding-item-info">
                            <div class="encoding-item-number" x-text="index + 1"></div>
                            <div class="encoding-item-details">
                                <div class="encoding-item-name" x-text="fileName"></div>

                                    </span>
                                    <template x-if="file.status === 'success'">
                                        <span class="meta-item">
                                            <span class="bi bi-arrow-right"></span>
                                            <span x-text="file.sizeEncoded"></span>
                                        </span>
                                    </template>
                                    <template x-if="file.dimensions &amp;&amp; file.status === 'success'">
                                        <span class="meta-item">
                                            <span class="bi bi-aspect-ratio"></span>
                                            <span x-text="`${file.dimensions.width}×${file.dimensions.height}`"></span>
                                        </span>
                                    </template>
                                </div>
                            </div>
                        </div>

                        <div class="encoding-item-actions" @click.stop="">
                            <div class="encoding-item-status">
                                <template x-if="file.status === 'success'">
                                    <span class="status-badge status-badge--success">
                                        <span class="bi bi-check-circle-fill"></span>
                                    </span>
                                </template>
                                <template x-if="file.status === 'error'">
                                    <span class="status-badge status-badge--error">
                                        <span class="bi bi-x-circle-fill"></span>
                                    </span>
                                </template>
                                <template x-if="file.status !== 'success' &amp;&amp; file.status !== 'error'">
                                    <span class="status-badge status-badge--processing">
                                        <span class="spinner-border spinner-border-sm"></span>
                                    </span>
                                </template>
                            </div>

                            <template x-if="file.status === 'success'">
                                <div class="action-buttons">
                                    <button type="button" @click="file.showCode = !file.showCode" class="action-btn action-btn--primary" :class="{ 'active': file.showCode }" title="Show code examples">
                                        <span class="bi" :class="file.showCode ? 'bi-chevron-up' : 'bi-code-slash'"></span>
                                        <span class="btn-text" x-text="file.showCode ? 'Hide' : 'Code'"></span>
                                    </button>
                                    <button type="button" @click="copyBaseStringToClipboard($event, file, 'data')" class="action-btn action-btn--secondary" title="Copy image data">
                                        <span class="bi bi-file-image"></span>
                                        <span class="btn-text">Image</span>
                                    </button>
                                    <button type="button" @click="copyBaseStringToClipboard($event, file, 'css')" class="action-btn action-btn--secondary" title="Copy CSS background">
                                        <span class="bi bi-braces"></span>
                                        <span class="btn-text">CSS</span>
                                    </button>
                                </div>
                            </template>
                            <template x-if="file.status === 'error'">
                                <div class="error-message" x-text="file.errorMessage"></div>
                            </template>
                        </div>
                    </div>

                    <div class="encoding-item-progress" x-show="file.status !== 'success' &amp;&amp; file.status !== 'error'" x-transition="">
                        <div class="progress-bar-container">
                            <div class="progress-bar-fill" :style="{ width: file.upload.progress + '%' }"></div>
                        </div>
                    </div>

                    <!-- Code Details Panel -->
                    <template x-if="file.status === 'success'">
                        <div class="encoding-item-details-panel" x-show="file.showCode" x-transition:enter="transition ease-out duration-200" x-transition:enter-start="opacity-0 transform -translate-y-2" x-transition:enter-end="opacity-100 transform translate-y-0" x-transition:leave="transition ease-in duration-150" x-transition:leave-start="opacity-100 transform translate-y-0" x-transition:leave-end="opacity-0 transform -translate-y-2" style="display: none;">

                            <div class="details-panel-content">
                                <!-- Preview -->
                                <div class="details-panel-header">
                                    <div class="details-preview">
                                        <img :src="file.base64?.data" :alt="fileName" class="preview-image">
                                    </div>
                                </div>

                                <!-- Code Examples -->
                                <div class="details-panel-codes">
                                    <div class="code-section">
                                        <div class="code-section-header">
                                            <h5 class="code-section-title">For use in &lt;img&gt; elements:</h5>
                                            <div class="code-section-actions">
                                                <button type="button" @click="selectTextInElement($el.parentElement.parentElement.nextElementSibling)" class="code-action-btn">
                                                    <span class="bi bi-cursor-text"></span>
                                                    Select all
                                                </button>
                                                <button type="button" @click="copyTextInElementToClipboard($event, $el.parentElement.parentElement.nextElementSibling)" class="code-action-btn">
                                                    <span class="bi bi-files"></span>
                                                    Copy
                                                </button>
                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                        <div class="code-area" x-text="file.base64?.data"></div>
                                    </div>

                                    <div class="code-section">
                                        <div class="code-section-header">
                                            <h5 class="code-section-title">For use as CSS background:</h5>
                                            <div class="code-section-actions">
                                                <button type="button" @click="selectTextInElement($el.parentElement.parentElement.nextElementSibling)" class="code-action-btn">

                                                    Select all

                                                </button>
                                            </div>
                                        </div>

                                    </div>
                                </div>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                    </template>
                </div>
            </template>
        </div>
    </div>

    <div class="row description content-box" style="margin-top: 25px;">
        <div class="col-lg-4 col-md-4 col-sm-4 col-xs-12">
            <h3 class="content-box-title">Supported file formats</h3>
            <p>
                Upload up to 20 images simultaneously (max. 1 MB each)
                in the most popular web formats: JPG, PNG, GIF, WebP, SVG, or BMP.
            </p>
            <p>
                Our converter handles everything from photos and graphics to icons and logos.
                Simply drag and drop your files or click to browse - the conversion happens
                instantly in your browser.
            </p>

                    <div class="col-lg-4 col-md-4 col-sm-4 col-xs-12">
                <h3 class="content-box-title">Image optimization option</h3>
                <p>
                    Enable smart compression for your JPEG &amp; PNG images to dramatically
                    reduce file sizes without sacrificing visual quality. Perfect for faster
                    page loads and reduced bandwidth usage.
                </p>
                <div class="optimization-toggle-container">

                        <input type="checkbox" name="optimize-images" id="optimize-images" wire:model="optimizeImages" class="optimization-toggle-input">

                        <span class="optimization-toggle-label">
                            <span class="bi bi-lightning-charge-fill"></span>
                            <span x-text="$wire.optimizeImages ? 'Optimization enabled' : 'Optimization disabled'"></span>

            <script async="" type="text/javascript" src="//cdn.carbonads.com/carbon.js?serve=CW7DV2QY&amp;placement=wwwbase64-imagede&amp;format=responsive" id="_carbonads_js"></script>

    <div class="row content-box" id="bsa-ads" style="margin-top: 25px;"></div>

    <div class="row content-box" style="margin-top: 25px;">
        <div class="col-lg-12">
            <h3 class="content-box-title">Why use Base64 Image Encoding?</h3>
        </div>

        <div class="col-lg-4 col-md-4 col-sm-6 col-xs-12">
            <h4 style="font-weight: 700; font-size: 18px; margin-top: 15px;">
                <i class="bi bi-lightning-charge" style="color: #2563eb;"></i>
                Reduce HTTP Requests
            </h4>
            <p>
                By embedding images directly into your HTML or CSS as base64 strings,
                you eliminate separate HTTP requests for image files. This can significantly
                improve page load times, especially for sites with many small images like
                icons or logos.
            </p>
        </div>

        <div class="col-lg-4 col-md-4 col-sm-6 col-xs-12">
            <h4 style="font-weight: 700; font-size: 18px; margin-top: 15px;">
                <i class="bi bi-shield-check" style="color: #10b981;"></i>
                Simplified Deployment
            </h4>
            <p>
                Base64 encoded images travel with your code, eliminating the need to manage
                separate image files and directories. This makes deployment simpler and
                reduces the risk of missing or broken image links in your application.
            </p>
        </div>

        <div class="col-lg-4 col-md-4 col-sm-6 col-xs-12">
            <h4 style="font-weight: 700; font-size: 18px; margin-top: 15px;">
                <i class="bi bi-envelope" style="color: #f59e0b;"></i>
                Perfect for Email Templates
            </h4>
            <p>
                Email clients often block external images by default. Base64 encoded images
                are embedded directly in your email HTML, ensuring your images display
                immediately without requiring user permission or external server access.
            </p>
        </div>

        <div class="col-lg-4 col-md-4 col-sm-6 col-xs-12">
            <h4 style="font-weight: 700; font-size: 18px; margin-top: 15px;">
                <i class="bi bi-code-square" style="color: #8b5cf6;"></i>
                Data URIs Support
            </h4>
            <p>
                All modern browsers support data URIs with base64 encoded images. Use them
                in img src attributes, CSS backgrounds, or even as favicon sources. They work
                seamlessly across different web technologies and frameworks.
            </p>
        </div>

        <div class="col-lg-4 col-md-4 col-sm-6 col-xs-12">
            <h4 style="font-weight: 700; font-size: 18px; margin-top: 15px;">
                <i class="bi bi-graph-up-arrow" style="color: #ec4899;"></i>
                Improved Caching
            </h4>
            <p>
                When images are embedded in your CSS or JavaScript files, they benefit from
                the same caching strategy as your code. This means fewer cache invalidation
                issues and more predictable performance across page visits.
            </p>
        </div>

        <div class="col-lg-4 col-md-4 col-sm-6 col-xs-12">
            <h4 style="font-weight: 700; font-size: 18px; margin-top: 15px;">
                <i class="bi bi-lock" style="color: #ef4444;"></i>
                No External Dependencies
            </h4>
            <p>
                Your images remain accessible even if CDN services are down or blocked.
                Base64 encoding ensures complete self-containment of your web application,
                improving reliability and reducing dependencies on external resources.
            </p>
        </div>
    </div>

</div><!-- /container -->
